#unusualrecipes #sweetpeppers #whitefish #vegetables \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This fish stew from land-locked Paraguay is usually made with a fish called 'dorado' (dolphin fish) which is found in the great Paraguay River, but\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1737\n|PortionCalories = 434\n|DatePublished=27th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 30 minutes\n |CookTime = 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Guiso de pescado (Fish stew) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Fish in dauphinoise potatoes</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Fabulous</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis [[Fish|fish]] [[Stew|stew]] from land-locked Paraguay is usually made with a fish called '[[dorado]]' (dolphin fish) which is found in the great Paraguay River, but any firm-fleshed [[white fish]] will be fine.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 [[Fish|fish]] steaks, weighing about 225g each\n| Seasoning\n| 60ml [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Vegetable|vegetable]] or [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 medium [[Onions|onions]], thinly sliced\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, crushed\n| 2 [[Tomatoes, peeled|tomatoes, peeled]] and sliced\n| 2 [[Sweet peppers|sweet peppers]], seeded and sliced\n| 2 medium [[Potatoes|potatoes]], peeled and thinly sliced\n| 1 [[Bay leaf|bay leaf]]\n| Sprig of [[Thyme|thyme]]\n| 2 or 3 sprigs [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| 140ml [[Dry white wine|dry white wine]]\n| 140ml [[Fish stock|fish stock]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the oven to 200\u00b0 C (400\u00b0 F - gas 6), [fan oven 180\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Guiso de pescado (Fish stew) baked.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Oven baked)\nImage:Guiso de pescado (Fish stew) ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The ingredients (for 2 people)\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Season the [[Fish|fish]] steaks, place in a dish and pour the [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] over them.\n| Allow to stand for an hour, turning occasionally.\n| Fry the [[onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] in a separate pan or a flame-proof casserole.\n| Layer the [[Fish|fish]] steaks, [[onions]], [[herbs]]  and [[Vegetables|vegetables]] in the [[Casserole|casserole]] and top with the sliced potatoes.\n| Season and and add the [[Wine|wine]] and [[Fish stock|fish stock]].\n| Drizzle with a little[[olive oil]]\n| Bake for 40 minutes, finishing under a hot grill for the last 5 minutes to crisp the potatoes.\n| Serve immediately.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nThis was a full meal and did not need any other accompaniment. \n===Chef's notes===\nWell this recipe turned out to be a bit of a trial. Following the original recipe, it was plain that there would not nearly enough liquid to cover the potatoes which meant that it could never be cooked on the hob. Adding more liquid to accommodate that would have turned it into soup.  \nI decided to oven cook it, except the oven broke down when I tried to use it, so the half finished dish had to be refrigerated and begun again the next day.  I decided to [[par boil]] the thinly sliced potatoes as I didn't want them to be undercooked.  Eventually it was a fantastic tasting (and looking) meal, but probably not as originally intended - the benefit of testing recipes first!\n\nThe recipe above is my modified version, you can see the original by viewing the ''history'' tab above.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Fish stew]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Fish stew]]\n[[Category:Paraguayan recipes|Fish stew]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Fish stew]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Fish stew]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes|Fish stew]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#fish #onions #oliveoil #fishstock #garlic #lemonjuice #parboil #unusualrecipes #sweetpeppers #whitefish #vegetables </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

#blender #garlic #olives #springonion #julienned #litres #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Lima beans are traditionally used to make this first course from Peru, but as they can be hard to find in the UK, use haricot beans instead\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}} \n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1330\n|PortionCalories = 221\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 2 hours + overnight\n |PrepTime = 30 minutes plus overnight soak\n |CookTime = 1 hour 30 minutes\n|Image = [[File:LimaBeans.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Try broad beans</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.9</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">They are close to Lima beans and taste better to my mind.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n[[Lima beans]] are traditionally used to make this first course from Peru, but as they can be hard to find in the UK, use [[Haricot beans|haricot beans]] instead.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 675 g [[Dried|dried]] haricot or baby [[Lima beans|lima beans]], soaked overnight\n| 1.9 [[Litres|litres]] water\n| 2 Dried [[Aj\u00ed pepper|aj\u00ed rojo chillies]], soaked and finely chopped\n| 1 tablespoon [[Grated|grated]] [[Ginger|ginger]]\n| A further 190 ml hot water \n| 340 g [[Kalamata]] [[Olives|olives]], stoned\n| A further 120 ml water, or as necessary\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, crushed\n| 10 large [[Spring onions|spring onions]], white part only, [[Julienned|julienned]], and soaked in iced water\n| 3 sticks [[Celery|celery]], [[Julienned|julienned]], and soaked in iced water\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon freshly-[[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]]\n| The [[Juice|juice]] of &frac12; a [[Lemon|lemon]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Drain the [[Beans|beans]] in a [[Colander|colander]] and combine them in a large saucepan with the 1.9 [[Litres|litres]] of water.\n| Bring up to the [[Boil|boil]], then reduce the heat so that the water is [[Simmering|simmering]]. \n| Cook the [[Beans|beans]], covered, for 35 to 40 minutes, or until just tender. Drain and set aside. \n| In a [[Blender|blender]], combine the [[Chillies|chillies]] and the [[Ginger|ginger]] with 190 ml of hot water and blend until smooth. Set the mixture aside. \n| Again in the [[Blender|blender]], mix the [[Olives|olives]] with the 120 ml of water, or just enough to make them move through the blades, and blend until completely smooth. Set this mixture aside. \n| In a large pan, heat the [[Olive oil|olive oil]] over medium heat. \n| Stir in the [[Garlic|garlic]], then immediately add the [[Chilli|chilli]]/[[Ginger|ginger]] mixture. \n| Cook for 10 minutes, stirring occasionally, until most of the liquid has evaporated. \n| Add the pur\u00e9ed [[Olive|olive]] mixture, reduce the heat to low, and cook for 5 minutes, stirring occasionally. Add the [[Beans|beans]] and continue cooking for 15 to 20 minutes, stirring gently every few minutes. \n| Remove from the heat, and allow to cool to room temperature. \n| When the [[Beans|beans]] are cool, drain the [[Spring onion|spring onion]] and [[Celery|celery]] and, in a small bowl, toss them with [[Salt|salt]], [[Pepper|pepper]], and [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]. \n| Serve the [[Beans|beans]] garnished with the [[Spring onion|spring onion]] and [[Celery|celery]].\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Habas en salsa de aceitunas (beans in olive sauce)]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Habas en salsa de aceitunas (beans in olive sauce)]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes|Habas en salsa de aceitunas (beans in olive sauce)]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Habas en salsa de aceitunas (beans in olive sauce)]]\n[[Category:Peruvian recipes|Habas en salsa de aceitunas (beans in olive sauce)]]\n[[Category:Starters|Habas en salsa de aceitunas (beans in olive sauce)]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Habas en salsa de aceitunas (beans in olive sauce)]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Habas en salsa de aceitunas (beans in olive sauce)]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beans #celery #ginger #limabeans #blender #garlic #olives #springonion #julienned #litres #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Hollywood Quesadillas, Vegetarian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#cheese #hollywoodquesadillas #diced #tortilla #salsa #pizza #quesadillas #peppers #jalapenos #tortillas #miseenplace \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=I first had these when working next door (from a bar on Sunset Blvd. in 1979)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1605\n|PortionCalories = 802\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = 2 as a snack\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 25 minutes (2 quesadillas)\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Hollywood Quesadillas recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Sound's fancy-pants</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Super tasty though</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nI first had these when working next door  (from a bar on Sunset Blvd. in 1979). The concept is simple, the ingredients simpler.I have enhanced the 'bar food' version, as I learned they could be more complete and more satisfying. Serve for snacks or a [[Light lunch|light lunch]]. Think of [[Quesadillas|quesadillas]] as [[Tex-Mex]] [[Pizza|pizza]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 [[Flour tortillas|flour tortillas]] (10\"-12\")\n| 6 oz. [[Grated|grated]] [[Monterey Jack cheese]]\n| 1/3 cup fresh green or red [[Jalapeno|jalapeno]] [[Peppers|peppers]],  seeded and membraned, then [[Diced|diced]] fine\n| &frac12; cup [[Diced|diced]] [[Spanish]] (Yellow) [[Onion|onion]], fine diced\n| 3 tablespoons [[Tomato salsa|tomato salsa]] ( or more) you choose the [[Salsa|salsa]]-I make my own)\n| Chopped [[Cilantro]] (opt.)\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Ground cumin|ground cumin]] (opt.)\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Have everything at or close to room temperature and a large [[Fry|fry]] pan!\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Spread all ingredients ( except [[Cheese|cheese]])with the back of a large spoon on [[Tortilla|tortilla]] one. Set [[Grill|grill]].hob to medium low..\n| Sprinkle [[Cheese|cheese]] over [[Tomato|tomato]] [[Pepper|pepper]] [[Salsa|salsa]]. Place second [[Tortilla|tortilla]] over top. slide this into the pan, and [[Steam|steam]] by using pan cover, or not if you want a more brittle version of [[Quesadillas|quesadillas]]. After about 5 minutes, flip the [[Quesadilla|quesadilla]] to [[Brown|brown]] tortilla 2. When it is all sizzling (3 minutes), transfer to cutting board and slice in [[Wedges|wedges]], as you would a [[Pizza|pizza]] or [[Cheesecake|cheesecake]], 3  or 4 to a plate.\n| This recipe can be multiplied for extra appetisers. Remember: you can put in refritos, [[Steamed|steamed]] [[Corn|corn]], chopped [[Olives|olives]]...but this is the core recipe.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with a good light 'cervesa' ([[Beer|beer]]) and lots of paper towels\n===Variations===\nChange [[Cheeses|cheeses]]. Medium Cheddars, Canadian Brick [[Cheese]] or Colby  also work well. You can also use chopped jarred [[Jalapenos|jalapenos]] or others, but it isn't fresh anymore. Canned jalapenos are milder, usually, then their fresh ancestors.\n===Chef's notes===\nOnly the [[Tortillas|tortillas]], [[Peppers|peppers]] and [[Cheese|cheese]] are constants.\n\nI found these difficult to flip, without emptying the contents all over the hob.  If you feel doubtful, use two plates to flip the quesadillas: Lay one over the pan, flip both over, place a second plate over the first, invert those, remove the top plate, replace with the pan, invert those, remove the plate.  ''If you can do a better job of explaining this, please do.''\n\nRecipe contributed by [[User:Tetramariner|Tetramariner]] 15:28, 30 January 2010 (GMT)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#cheese #hollywoodquesadillas #diced #tortilla #salsa #pizza #quesadillas #peppers #jalapenos #tortillas #miseenplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Home-made Churros",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Home-made Churros, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#churrera #frozen #homemadechurros #greaseproofpaper #deepfatfryer #flour #icingsugar #boiling #potato #orceserranohams #cuporjug \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A churro is a fried-dough pastry-based snack, sometimes made from potato dough, originated in Spain, and is popular in Latin America, France, Portugal\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 120\n|PortionCalories = 24\n|DatePublished=8th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 5\n|Difficulty = 2\n|ImageComment = Churros and chocolate\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 5 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Churros recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">One is enough!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">2</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">These are more unhealthy than deep-fried Mars Bars.  Yuk!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nA churro is a fried-dough pastry-based snack, sometimes made from [[potato]] dough, originated in Spain, and is popular in Latin America, France, Portugal, the USA, and Spanish-speaking Caribbean islands. It is sometimes referred to as a Spanish doughnut or Mexican doughnut. The snack gets its name from its shape, which resembles the horns of the Churro breed of sheep reared in the Spanish grasslands of Huarocho. There are two types of churros in Spain. One is long and fat and the other, specially popular in Madrid, is thin and knotted (porra). They both are normally eaten for breakfast dipped in hot chocolate (drink).\nThe churro is typically fried to a crunchy consistency and sometimes sprinkled with [[sugar]]. Its surface is ridged due to being piped from a [[churrera]], a syringe with a star-shaped nozzle.\n\nLike [[pretzels]], churros are often sold by street vendors who in many cases will fry them freshly on the street stand and sell them hot. In Spain and Mexico, they are available in cafes for breakfast, although they may be found throughout the day and night as a snack.\n\nVery popular for breakfast, churros are a simple type of doughnut.  They can be made with a [[churrera]], obtainable from [http://www.delicioso.co.uk/ Delicioso] and [[Orce Serrano Hams]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| Measuring in a [[cup or jug]], you need equal volumes of [[Plain flour|plain flour]] and water, so for this recipe measure 500 ml of both\n| Large pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| [[Olive]] or [[Sunflower oil|sunflower oil]]\n| Caster or [[Icing sugar|icing sugar]] (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the water and [[Salt|salt]] in a saucepan and bring to the [[Boil|boil]].\n| [[Sieve]] the [[Flour|flour]] into a bowl.\n| Add the [[Boiling|boiling]] water to the [[Flour|flour]] and mix thoroughly with a fork.  The mixture should be like a thick paste.\n| Do not worry too much about any lumps as the force on the churrera will disperse them.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large [[Deep frying|deep frying]] or saut\u00e9 pan.\n| Force the mixture into the [[churrera]] as tightly as you can, to reduce the amount of air in the mixture.\n| When the [[Oil|oil]] is almost [[Smoking|smoking]], pipe the dough into the pan, either in a spiral or in longish strips.  \n| Cook until they are a rich golden [[Brown|brown]].  Because they float, you will need to turn them over to ensure even cooking.  This is best done with either [[skewers]] or chopsticks.\n| If they are spiral shaped, cut them into long pieces with scissors.\n| Sprinkle them with [[Sugar|sugar]] if desired\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Churros ready to be frozen.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Churros ready to be frozen\nImage:Cooked, frozen, home-made churros.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Home-made, frozen and cooked churros\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with a cup of thick dark drinking [[Chocolate|chocolate]] into which the churros are dunked.  Unless you have quite a sweet tooth, I would avoid sprinkling them with the [[Sugar|sugar]].\n\nThis recipe makes 10 large churros.  Allow 2-3 per person.\n\n===Variations===\nThe above is a very basic recipe and in my experience the more usual one.  However, sometimes [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and/or [[Eggs|eggs]] are included.\n\nAlthough they would lose their authenticity, you can play around with them and add any flavourings you like.  I have made them with [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Paprika|paprika]] before.\n\n===Chef's tip===\nYou can use a [[deep fat fryer]] to cook the churros, but it is quite difficult to pipe in the mixture if your fryer is a long thin one.  They would probably work better in a round fryer.\n\nAs an alternative to a [[churrera]], it is possible to make them using a [[piping bag]] with a large star-shaped nozzle, although not quite so easy.\n\nChurros can be [[Frozen|frozen]].  Pipe them onto [[greaseproof paper]], or preferably [[Bake-O-Glide]] - it can be quite tricky extracting them from [[greaseproof paper]]. [[Open freeze]] them until they are hard (several hours), then put them into bags.  They should be cooked directly from [[frozen]].  If they are [[frozen]], they are easier to cook in a [[deep fat fryer]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Churros]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Churros]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n[[Category:Cuban recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#churrera #frozen #homemadechurros #greaseproofpaper #deepfatfryer #flour #icingsugar #boiling #potato #orceserranohams #cuporjug </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Homemade tortilla chips",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Homemade tortilla chips, Vegetarian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#corntortillas #homemadetortillachips #vegetableoil #chips #tortillachips #oliveoil #masaharina #panfried #corntortillarecipe #salsa #fry \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Tortilla chips are made by shallow frying soft corn tortillas - these instructions just cover the frying part so can hardly be considered a recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1342\n|PortionCalories = 671\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 2\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = None\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Homemade tortilla chips recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love this.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Brilliant idea.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]]</span></span>\n}}\n\n[[Tortilla chips]] are made by shallow [[Frying|frying]] soft [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]] - these instructions just cover the frying part so can hardly be considered a recipe!\n\nIf you want to start from scratch, [[Corn tortilla recipe|use this recipe]] to make the soft corn tortillas yourself.  It's the [[masa harina]] that gives them that unique flavour.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| &#189; cup of [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 1 pack of soft [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]] (8 to 10 tortillas)\n| Fine [[Salt|salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cut the each [[Corn tortillas|corn tortilla]] into 6 triangles\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large heavy based [[Frying pan|frying pan]] over a medium heat.\n| Add the triangles in small batches and [[Fry|fry]] for about a minute or until they just start to [[Brown|brown]].  You need to be quick as they can burn easily.\n| Lift the cooked [[Chips|chips]] out of the pan and let the [[Oil|oil]] drain and then stack on paper towels to remove excess oil.\n| Sprinkle with a pinch of [[Salt|salt]].\n| Allow to cool and crisp-up a little before serving.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nTry one of our [[Salsa|salsa recipes]] or this [[Tex-Mex bean dip for tacos]].\n===Chef's notes===\nFor health reasons, I have used [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n\nYou could possibly fry the whole tortilla first and then cut into triangles as they remain soft for a ref minutes after frying.  I will try that next time I make these.\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#corntortillas #homemadetortillachips #vegetableoil #chips #tortillachips #oliveoil #masaharina #panfried #corntortillarecipe #salsa #fry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It is very easy to prepare and the ingredients are also easy to find. \n\n===You will need:===\n* Fried [[whole tortillas]]\n* ground (minced) [[meat]] (as needed)\n* [[Pico de gallo]] (as needed) \n* [[boiled eggs]] (one slice per enchilada)\n* [[salsa]] (as desired)\n\n===Procedure:===\nPrepare the ground meat as desired, once the meat is ready all what you have to do is assemble the enchiladas. Grab the tortilla and cover it with the meat. Use the pico de gallo as your topping. Cut the boiled eggs into slices and top each enchilada with once slice. Finally, pour the salsa over the enchilada and you are done!\n\nEnjoy!\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n{{BottomBanner}}\n{{RecipeSkip}}\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#honduranenchiladas #salsa #spicyrecipes #picodegallo #boiledeggs #latinamericanrecipes #wholetortillas #recipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

From its home in Mexico, the dish has spread throughout the Americas.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 tablespoons (45ml) [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| A pinch [[Chili powder|chili powder]]\n| 4 [[Plum|plum]] [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], peeled, seeded and chopped\n| 2 [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]]\n| 2 [[free range eggs]]\n| Chopped [[Chilli peppers|chilli peppers]], to taste\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]], to taste\n| 1 tablespoon freshly chopped [[Coriander|coriander]] or [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| To prepare the ranchero sauce, in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]], heat 1 tablespoon [[Oil|oil]] over medium heat\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]], and saut\u00e9 until softened, 4 or 5 minutes\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Peppers|peppers]], [[Chili powder|chili powder]], [[Salt|salt]] and a few grinds of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and reduce to a [[Simmer|simmer]]\n| [[Simmer]] for about 10 minutes, until the [[Sauce|sauce]] begins to thicken\n| Add the [[Coriander|coriander]] or [[Parsley|parsley]], turn off the heat and cover the pan to keep the [[Sauce|sauce]] warm\n| In another [[Frying pan|frying pan]], lightly [[Fry|fry]] the [[Tortillas|tortillas]] in 1 tablespoon of [[Oil|oil]]. Remove and drain\n| If necessary, add additional [[Oil|oil]] to the second [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Eggs|eggs]] until they are \"[[How to fry an egg|sunny-side up]]\". \n| Transfer the [[Eggs|eggs]] to the [[Tortillas|tortillas]], and cover with the ranchero sauce\n| Serve immediately\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#huevosrancheros #eggs #tomatoes #tortillas #fry #simmer #chilipowder #onion #sauce #parsley #garlic </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

corn g sweetcorn ml corn oil\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1947\n|PortionCalories = 194\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Humitas (Sweetcorn tamales)\n |Servings = Serves 10 - Makes 10 tamales\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 40 minutes\n |CookTime = 35 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Humitas (Sweetcorn tamales) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">I can never make these work</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">2.5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Can you?</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nAn unusual [[Tamales|tamales]] recipe from Chiclayo which is the capital city of the Lambayeque region in northern Peru.\n\n\n'''For the [[Corn|corn]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 900 g [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]]\n| 15 ml [[Corn|corn]] [[Oil|oil]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Achiote|achiote]] granules, dissolved in 10 ml hot [[Corn|corn]] [[Oil|oil]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| Pinch of [[Pepper|pepper]]\n}}\n'''For the humitas'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 20 [[Corn husks|corn husks]]\n| 1 dried yellow [[Aj\u00ed pepper|aj\u00ed pepper]], rehydrated in hot water and sliced into 10 pieces\n| 10 [[Black olives|black olives]], cut in half\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], finely sliced\n| &frac14; teaspoon [[Achiote|achiote]] granules, dissolved in 5 ml hot [[Corn|corn]] [[Oil|oil]]\n| Pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| 450 g skinless, boneless [[Chicken|chicken]] breasts, cut into ten pieces\n| 2 [[Eggs, hard-boiled]], peeled and cut into 10 slices each\n| Nylon thread or raffia\n}}\n===Method===\n\n\n'''For the [[Corn|corn]]:'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Blend the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] into a rough [[Mash|mash]].\n| Place in a bowl and mix in the remaining [[Corn|corn]] ingredients.\n| Leave for at least 30 minutes to thicken.\n}}\n'''For the humitas:'''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Take 2 [[Corn husks|corn husks]] and lay them so that half of one lies on the half of the other.\n| Place 2 good tablespoons of the [[Corn|corn]] mixture in the centre of the husks.\n| To a small [[Frying pan|frying pan]], on a low heat, add the aj\u00ed, [[Olives|olives]], [[Onion|onion]], [[Achiote|achiote]] [[Oil|oil]] and [[Salt|salt]].\n| [[Fry]], stirring constantly, for a couple of minutes.\n| Remove from heat and allow to cool.\n| For each humita, make a dent in the centre of the [[Corn|corn]] mix and add 1 [[Chicken|chicken]] piece and one slice of [[Egg|egg]].\n| From the [[Fried|fried]] mixture, add a slice of aj\u00ed, 2 [[Olive|olive]] halves and a few [[Onion|onion]] slices.\n| Put a further 2 tablespoons of the [[Corn|corn]] mixture on the top and press the whole thing into a rectangle.\n| Fold one [[Corn husk|corn husk]] over the mixture and the other husk over that.\n| Tie one of the open ends with the nylon thread or raffia, about 5 cm from the end.\n| Do the same with the other end and wrap the humita lengthwise with the thread.\n| When all of the humitas have been made, place them in a wide pan (or two separate ones) so that they all lie on the base of the pan.\n| Add enough hot water to just cover the humitas, cover, and [[Boil|boil]] for 20 minutes.\n| Unfold the humitas and serve warm.\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nCorn husks can be obtained from '''[[Cool Chile Co]]''' and yellow (amarillo) aj\u00ed chillies are sold by '''[http://www.southdevonchillifarm.co.uk/shop/index.php?target=products&product_id=158 The South Devon Chilli Farm]'''\n==See also==\n* {{See also - Jointing a chicken}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Humitas (sweetcorn tamales)]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Humitas (sweetcorn title": "Jicama, chili and lime salad",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Jicama, chili and lime salad a vegetarian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#jicama #limes #chilepiquin #jicamachiliandlimesalad #speedpeeler #appetiser #juice #chineseturnip #refrigerate #zest #lime \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This crispy, tangy salad makes a good side-dish or an appetiser to serve with drinks. You will be able to get jicama from specialist Mexican suppliers\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 298\n|PortionCalories = 74\n|DatePublished=12th April 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = thumb|right|Jicama roots\n |Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 10 minutes (to chill)\n |PrepTime = 1 hour, 10 minutes\n |CookTime = None\n |Image = [[Image:Jicama roots.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Can't find Jicama here \u2639\ufe0f</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">It's a shame because I'd love to try this.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The&nbsp;Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis crispy, tangy [[Salad|salad]] makes a good side-dish or an [[Appetiser|appetiser]] to serve with drinks.\n\nYou will be able to get [[Jicama|jicama]] from specialist [[Tex-Mex|Mexican suppliers]] and [[Oriental suppliers]] where you will often find it marked as [[Chinese turnip]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 [[Jicama]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 2 fresh [[Chile piquin|bird chillies]]\n| 2 [[Limes|limes]], one zested and juiced, the other cut into wedges.\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Peel the [[Jicama|jicama]] with a [[Potato peeler|potato peeler]] or a [[Speed peeler|speed peeler]] and cut into 2 cm 93/4 cubes)\n| Add these to a serving bowl sprinkle with the [[Salt|salt]].\n| Scrape the seeds out of the [[Chile piquin|chillies]] and cut them into very thin strips.\n| Remove the [[Zest|zest]] from one of the [[Limes|limes]] and sprinkle over the cubes.  Squeeze the [[Juice|juice]] from this [[Lime|lime]] and add to the mixture.\n| Toss the mixture really well to mix evenly.\n| [[Refrigerate]] for an hour then serve with [[Lime wedges|lime wedges]] and cocktail sticks.\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Oriental cuisine]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#jicama #limes #chilepiquin #jicamachiliandlimesalad #speedpeeler #appetiser #juice #chineseturnip #refrigerate #zest #lime </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Locro",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Locro a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#locro #potatodumplings #mozzarellacheese #sweetcorn #tinfoil #chorizo #beef #onions #tortillachips #tomatoes #yellowcornmeal \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Locro is a hearty thick stew popular along the Andes mountain range\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 4492\n|PortionCalories = 748\n|DatePublished=3rd November 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Plain [[tortilla chips]] were a perfect accompaniment for this.\n |Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 3 hours 20 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 3 hours\n |Image = [[Image:Locro recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">My Masa Fix is here!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.7</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Anything Mexcian is good by me.  Love the Teviot pie idea</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nLocro is a hearty thick [[Stew|stew]] popular along the Andes mountain range. The dish is a classic Ecuadorian [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Potato|potato]] [[Soup|soup]] from the Ecuadorian cuisine. This is also a dish in Peruvian cuisine, which at one point held the centre of the Inca empire. It typical also in Argentina prepared by the different native Indian tribes at the time of the [[Spanish]] conquest. Its origin [[Dates|dates]] to before the Spanish colonial times.\n\nThe defining ingredients are [[Corn|corn]], some form of [[Meat|meat]] (usually [[Beef|beef]], but sometimes [[Beef jerky|beef jerky]] or [[Chorizo|chorizo]]), and [[Vegetables|vegetables]]. Other ingredients vary widely, and typically include [[Onion|onion]], [[Beans|beans]], [[Squash|squash]] or [[Pumpkin|pumpkin]]. It is mainly eaten in winter.\n\nIn some parts, such as in the Santiago del Estero Province of Argentina, a red hot sauce made from red peppers and paprika known as [[quiquirimichi]] is served on the side.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| 2 large [[Onions|onions]], peeled and sliced\n| 4 [[Cloves garlic, peeled and crushed|cloves garlic, peeled and crushed]]\n| 750 g (1.5 lb) [[Beef|beef]] [[Stewing|stewing]] [[Steak|steak]], cut into cubes\n| 1 x 400g (14 oz) can of peeled [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of ground white [[cumin]]\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of dried [[oregano]]\n| 1 teaspoon freshly ground [[coriander]] seeds\n| 1 bay leaf\n| Juice from 1/2 a lemon\n| 150 ml (1/4 pint) [[Beef Stock|beef stock]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Paprika powder|paprika powder]]\n| &#189; of a teaspoon of [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]], or to taste.\n| 1 x 400g (14 oz) can of [[Chickpeas|chickpeas]], rinsed and drained\n| 125 g whole [[Chorizo sausage|chorizo sausage]], sliced thickly\n| 200 g can of [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]], rinsed and drained\n| 75 g [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]] cut into cubes\n| [[Salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to taste\n| 2 tablespoons of [[masa harina]] or [[yellow cornmeal]], optional thickening.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Locro simmering.jpg|Seal the lid with [[tin foil]] to prevent the stew from drying out\nImage:Locro pie.jpg|Locro pie with [[potato dumplings]]\nImage:Locro pie oven-ready.jpg|Locro pie with [[potato dumplings]], ready for the oven\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large pan or [[Dutch Oven|Dutch oven]] and saut\u00e9 the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] for 4 minutes or until softened and slightly coloured.\n| Reserve the onions, increase the heat and brown the beef, a handful of pieces at a time.\n| Add the onions back to the pan, together with the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and their juice. Also add the [[lemon juice]], [[Stock|stock]], ground spices, [[Paprika|paprika]], [[Chili powder|chili powder]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]. \n| Bring to the [[Boil|boil]] then cover and [[Simmer|simmer]] for 2 hours.\n| Stir in the cornmeal to thicken if needed. Add the [[Chorizo|chorizo]], [[Chick peas|chick peas]] and [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] and [[Simmer|simmer]] for a further 30 minutes\n| Transfer to serving bowls and dot with pieces of [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with crusty [[Bread|bread]].\n\nI'm not sure about the authenticity, but plain [[tortilla chips]] were a marvellous accompaniment to this dish.\n===Chef's notes===\nI find it useful to use a few layers of scrunched-up [[tin foil]] under the lid to seal the pot because this prevents the contents from drying out when [[simmering]] for long periods of time.\n===Variations===\nWe used the (frozen) second half of the locro to make a sort of South-American [[Teviot pie]]!  Whilst not the least bit authentic, it was rather delicious.  The [[potato dumplings]] were rolled in [[yellow cornmeal]] and laid on the top of the locro and covered with slices of [[mozzarella cheese]].  This was oven baked for 30 minutes or so at 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4).\n===See also===\n* {{ChiliConCarne}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Ecuadorian recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Peruvian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Soup and stock recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]][[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#locro #potatodumplings #mozzarellacheese #sweetcorn #tinfoil #chorizo #beef #onions #tortillachips #tomatoes #yellowcornmeal </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]

It is one of the most popular recipes in Peru.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 pounds (900g) of [[Beef tenderloin|beef tenderloin]] or other tender [[Steak|steak]]\n| &frac14; cup [[Red wine|red wine]], e.g., Burgundy\n| 2 tablespoons of Crushed [[Garlic|garlic]]\n| 2 medium [[Onions|onions]] cut in strips\n| 4 [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Seeds|seeds]] removed, pur\u00e9ed in a [[Blender|blender]]\n| 5 [[Potatoes|potatoes]] peeled and cut into strips for [[Frying|frying]]\n| 1 yellow [[Peruvian chili pepper|chili pepper (aji)]] cut into thin strips\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Vinegar|vinegar]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]]\n| [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n| [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n| culantro (or substitute with [[Coriander|coriander]])\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cut the [[Meat|meat]] into thin strips and [[Marinate|marinate]] them in the [[Wine|wine]] for 1 hour.\n| Use a [[Wok|wok]] to cook [[Garlic|garlic]] in [[Oil|oil]] over medium heat and add the [[Meat|meat]]. Reserve the [[Juice|juice]].\n| Add the [[Tomato|tomato]] pur\u00e9e, [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]. Cook a few minutes.\n| Add the [[Soy sauce|soy sauce]] while stirring the [[Meat|meat]] in the [[Wok|wok]].\n| Add the [[Onions|onions]], aji strips, [[Cilantro|cilantro]] and [[Vinegar|vinegar]]. Combine the [[Juice|juice]] from the [[Meat|meat]].\n| [[Fry]] the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] in a separate pan and add to the other ingredients.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe the dish with [[White rice|white rice]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Stir fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#lomosaltado #vinegar #potatoes #onions #steak #wok #juice #soysauce #frying #garlic #whiterice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

</span></span>\n\n\n}}\nWhen these [[Pancakes|pancakes]] are made large they are good as a [[Main course|main course]], topped with [[spicy chicken]] & [[Sour cream|sour cream]], [[Grilled|grilled]] [[Starters|starters]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 medium [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| 160g [[Masa harina|masa harina]]\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and [[Grated|grated]]\n| 1 Clove of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 200g [[Cheddar cheese]]\n| Pinch of [[Chilli powder|chilli powder]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]] to taste\n| [[Vegetable oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* [[Boil]] the [[Potatoes|potatoes]], whole, in their skins until cooked, rub the skins off and [[Mash|mash]] them.\n* Grate the [[Cheese|cheese]] and [[Onion|onion]]\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add all of the ingredients to a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a [[Dough|dough]] hook or a plastic blade and [[Kneading bread|knead]] into a fairly firm dough, add a little water or more [[Masa harina|masa harina]] to adjust the consistency\n| Rest for 30 minutes then roll out into 1 cm thick [[Pancakes|pancakes]]\n| Shallow [[Fry|fry]] in [[Oil|oil]] until golden [[Brown|brown]] and crispy, turning now and again.\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Mexican fishballs frying.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Frying the fishballs\nImage:Mexican fishballs in tomato sauce ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The original ingredients - the recipe has since been slightly modified\nImage:Mexican potato cake frying.jpg|thumb|300px|right|You can probably use more oil, but I like to keep it down as these can be sponges for fat\nImage:Mexican potato cake dough.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Firm dough, ready to rest\n</gallery>\n===Chef's notes===\nMaking this (for about 8 people), I used about 200 g [[masa harina]] and 800 g [[desire potatoes]], weighed after boiling and peeling.  A dusting of [[yellow cornmeal]] makes them easy to roll and a nice finish.\n\nThe mixture kept well for 4 days, refrigerated in a Lock&Lock box and made really nice sized nibbles by rolling into balls (golf-ball sized), pressing in a [[tortilla-press]] then [[shallow-frying]].\n\nIf you don't have a [[tortilla press]], use 2 chopping boards or just two sheets of wood as a substitute.  Place ball of [[dough]] between two non-stick surfaces such as small squares of [[Bake-O-Glide]] and stand on them!\n===Suppliers===\nSee the [[Tortilla Press]] page for UK suppliers.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#mexicanpotatocakes #masaharina #pancakes #dough #potatoes #onion #tortillapress #cheese #spicychicken #grilled #miseenplace </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It works with [[chicken]] as well as [[beef]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 packet of [[corn flour tortillas]] or [[wheat flour tortillas]]\n| 225 g (1/2 lb) lean minced [[beef]]\n| 1 tablespoon smoked [[jalapeno pepper]]\n* 1/4 of a teaspoon of [[black peppercorns]]\n* 5 cm (1/2\") [[cinnamon stick]]\n* 1 teaspoon [[white cumin]] seeds\n* 1 teaspoon [[black cumin]] seeds\n* 1/2 a teaspoon of flavours to mingle\n| Heat the [[ghee]] in a [[frying]] pan or [[wok]]\n| Add the mince and [[fry]]  until done to your liking\n| Pour off any excess [[fat]]\n| Add the juice from half an [[orange]], bubbles\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe with any or all of the following: [[sour cream]], [[guacamole]], [[pickled jalape\u00f1os]], a  green salad, [[grapefruit salsa]], chopped mince.\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Main title": "Mote with dried peaches",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Mote with dried peaches recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#dried #peaches #wheat #motewithdriedpeaches #huesillos #honey #drink #huesillo #chile #fridge #cinnamonstick \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Mote con huesillo is a traditional Chilean summer-time drink known as the refreshing national drink It is a non-alcoholic beverage consisting of a\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1944\n|PortionCalories = 324\n|DatePublished=10th April 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 13 hours 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 13 hours\n |CookTime = 30 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Mote with dried peaches recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Too sweet for my taste!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">3.8</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">You may love it though!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nMote con huesillo is a traditional [[Chile]]an summer-time [[Drink|drink]], known as the refreshing national drink. It is a non-alcoholic beverage consisting of a sweet liquid syrup made with [[Dried|dried]] [[Peaches|peaches]] (huesillo) and mixed with fresh cooked husked [[Wheat|wheat]] (mote).\n\nThe sweet syrup is made with [[Sugar|sugar]], however can be supplemented with [[Honey|honey]]. When the drink is served without the dried peaches, it is called a descarozados. Both the mote and [[huesillo]] correspond to Mediterranean climates, like that of central Chile.\nThis drink is very popular during summer months and is sold by street vendors on rolling carts or stands. It is also a very popular homemade recipe, for which the ingredients are readily available in supermarkets, small grocery stores and farmers' markets. Bottled, canned or store packaged versions of mote con huesillo are limited and less common.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 12 whole [[Dried|dried]] [[Peaches|peaches]]\n| 150 g [[Sugar]] or molasses / golden syrup\n| [[Cinnamon stick]]\n| 250 g (&frac14; lb.) husked [[Wheat|wheat]]\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\nThe huesillos, or [[Dried|dried]] [[Peaches|peaches]], are washed and soaked the night prior to preparation in order to rehydrate them.\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cook the [[Dried|dried]] [[Peaches|peaches]] for thirty minutes in a [[Sugar|sugar]], molasses, or golden syrup and water mixture, with some natural [[Cinnamon sticks|cinnamon sticks]].\n| To give the [[Drink|drink]] its [[Honey|honey]] hue, sugar is heated in a [[Sauce|sauce]] pan in order to caramelise it and bring it to a rich [[Orange|orange]] ruby colour, which is added to the syrup mixture (this step is not necessary if you have used molasses or golden syrup).\n| While the [[huesillos]] are cooking, the mote, or husked [[Wheat|wheat]], is cooked in water until tender. \n| Once the mote are cooked, they are drained and added to the [[huesillos]] and syrup, and left to cool.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nThis combination is served chilled, in a tall glass with a tall dessert spoon for easy serving.\n\nServe it in a half-a-litre glass previously cold from the [[Fridge|fridge]] and which had been standing upside down on top of a dish with a [[Sugar|sugar]] base.\n\n===Variations===\nSome people have used [[Prunes|prunes]] instead of [[Dried|dried]] [[Peaches|peaches]], but it is definitely not the same!\n\n''This recipe was added by [[User:Mv.valdivia|Maria Veronica]], one of our Chilean visitors.''\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilean recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Drink and beverage recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#dried #peaches #wheat #motewithdriedpeaches #huesillos #honey #drink #huesillo #chile #fridge #cinnamonstick </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

title": "Mozzarella bites",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Mozzarella bites a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#egg #breadcrumbs #mozzarellabites #cheese #starter #miseenplace #deepfried #deepfatfryer #snack #mozzarella #mozzarellacheese \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Recipe for deep fried mozzarella bites, a great starter or just a tasty snack\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 706\n|PortionCalories = 353\n|DatePublished=8th March 2014\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Mozzarella bites recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wow!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">These look fabulous.</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:NonLoggedInUser|NonLoggedInUser]] </span></span>\n}}\nRecipe for [[Deep fried|deep fried]] [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] bites, a great [[Starter|starter]] or just a tasty [[Snack|snack]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 113g (\u00bc pound) [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]], drained\n| 118 ml (\u00bd cup) seasoned [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]]\n| 1 large [[Egg|egg]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat [[Deep fat fryer|deep fat fryer]] to 175\u00b0C (350\u00b0F)\n\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Preheat deep fryer to 350\u00b0F (175\u00b0C).\n| Slice mozzarella into cubes 2-3 cm on a side.\n| In a small bowl, whisk [[Egg|egg]].\n| Fill another small bowl with [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]].\n| Dip 5-6 bites at a time into the [[Egg|egg]].\n| Shake excess [[Egg|egg]] off the bites and place them in the [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]].\n| Shake bowl of [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]], evenly coating all bites. Add more [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]] as needed.\n| Place coated bites to the side and repeat for remaining bites.\n| After all bites have been coated, repeat the [[Egg|egg]]-[[Dip|dip]] and [[Crumb|crumb]]-coat for each once more.\n| Place all bites in fryer basket and submerge in 175\u00b0C [[Oil|oil]].\n| Let sit for 30 seconds, gently rocking basket occasionally.\n| Lift basket and let cool for a few seconds. If [[Cheese|cheese]] is not beginning to ooze out from half the sticks, re-submerge in [[Oil|oil]] for another 10-15 seconds, gently shaking the basket. Repeat until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is just starting to ooze out.\n| Dump onto [[Paper towel|paper towel]] and pat off excess [[Oil|oil]] gently.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* [http://en.wikibooks.org/wiki/Cookbook:Mozzarella_Sticks Wiki cookbook]\n===Variations===\nTry [[Mozzarella sticks]], identical recipe but the result is breaded cheese sticks rather than bites.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#egg #breadcrumbs #mozzarellabites #cheese #starter #miseenplace #deepfried #deepfatfryer #snack #mozzarella #mozzarellacheese </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

title": "Mozzarella sticks",

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Mozzarella sticks a cheese recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#egg #breadcrumbs #mozzarellasticks #cheese #mozzarella #deepfried #dip #snack #crumb #mozzarellacheese #starter \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Recipe for deep fried mozzarella sticks, a great starter or just a tasty snack\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 706\n|PortionCalories = 353\n|DatePublished=8th March 2014\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime =  20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  15 minutes\n|CookTime =  5 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Mozzarella Sticks recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Oh, love these</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Crunchy, cheesy and gooey. Mmm!</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nRecipe for [[Deep fried|deep fried]] [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] sticks, a great [[Starter|starter]] or just a tasty [[Snack|snack]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 113g (\u00bc pound) [[Mozzarella cheese|mozzarella cheese]], drained\n| 118 ml (\u00bd cup) seasoned [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]]\n| 1 large [[Egg|egg]]\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* Preheat [[Deep fat fryer|deep fat fryer]] to 175\u00b0C (350\u00b0F)\n\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Preheat deep fryer to 350\u00b0F (175\u00b0C).\n| Slice [[Mozzarella|mozzarella]] into sticks 1-3 cm in diameter.\n| In a small bowl, whisk [[Egg|egg]].\n| Fill another small bowl with [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]].\n| Dip 3-4 sticks at a time into the [[Egg|egg]].\n| Shake excess [[Egg|egg]] off sticks and place them in the [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]].\n| Shake bowl of [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]], evenly coating all sticks. Add more [[Bread crumbs|bread crumbs]] as needed.\n| Place coated sticks to the side and repeat for remaining sticks.\n| After all sticks have been coated, repeat the [[Egg|egg]]-[[Dip|dip]] and [[Crumb|crumb]]-coat for each once more.\n| Place all sticks in fryer basket and submerge in 175\u00b0C [[Oil|oil]].\n| Let sit for 30 seconds, gently rocking basket occasionally.\n| Lift basket and let cool for a few seconds. If [[Cheese|cheese]] is not beginning to ooze out from half the sticks, re-submerge in [[Oil|oil]] for another 10-15 seconds, gently shaking the basket. Repeat until the [[Cheese|cheese]] is just starting to ooze out.\n| Dump onto [[Paper towel|paper towel]] and pat off excess [[Oil|oil]] gently.\n}}\n===Recipe source===\n\n* [http://en.wikibooks.org/wiki/Cookbook:Mozzarella_Sticks Wiki cookbook]\n===Variations===\nTry [[Mozzarella bites]], identical recipe but the result is bite-sized nibbles, rather than sticks.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Italian recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#egg #breadcrumbs #mozzarellasticks #cheese #mozzarella #deepfried #dip #snack #crumb #mozzarellacheese #starter </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

-->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3314\n|PortionCalories = 414\n|DatePublished=21st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 8 - Makes 8 [[Tamales|tamales]]\n |Difficulty = 3\n |ImageComment = An assembled nacatamal\n |TotalTime = 4 hours 25 minutes\n |PrepTime = 25 minutes plus overnight marinade\n |CookTime = 4 hours\n |Image = [[Image:Nacatamal (Nicaraguan tamales) recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Tha looks good Julia</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Is filling:'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 450 g boneless [[pork]], [[Chicken|chicken]] pieces or [[Turkey|turkey]] breast, cut into 8 pieces\n| 70 ml [[Seville orange]] [[Juice|juice]] or 35 ml each of [[Orange|orange]] and [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Achiote|achiote]]\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, crushed\n}}\n'''For the [[Masa|masa]]:'''\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 450 g [[Tamale|tamale]] [[Flour|flour]] or [[Masa harina|masa harina]]\n| 280 ml [[Milk|milk]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Lard|lard]] or Trex\n| 15 ml [[Seville orange]] [[Juice|juice]] or a mixture of [[Orange|orange]] and [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Salt|salt]]\n| 115 g [[Mashed potato|mashed potato]]\n}}\n\n'''Garnishes:'''\n\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 [[Potato]], raw, sliced thinly into 5 cm squares\n| 2 [[Tomatoes]], thinly sliced\n| 2 [[Onions]], thinly sliced\n| 2 [[Sweet peppers]], thinly sliced\n| [[Mint leaves]]\n| 8 teaspoons of raw [[Rice|rice]]\n| [[Chillies]], thinly sliced\n}}\n'''For wrapping:'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 8 sheets of [[Tin-foil|tin-foil]], cut into 38-40 cm squares \n}}\n'''OR'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| [[Corn husks]]\n}}\n'''OR'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| [[Banana leaves]]\n}}\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the filling ingredients and leave to [[Marinate|marinate]] overnight.\n| Mix the [[Masa|masa]] ingredients in a saucepan and cook over medium heat until the mixture is firm, but remains moist - about 30 minutes.\n| Take one-eighth of the [[Masa|masa]] and place in the centre of one piece [[Foil|foil]] or a husk.\n| Push 2 slices of [[Potato|potato]] into the [[Masa|masa]] near the bottom, then one piece of [[Meat|meat]] in the centre.\n| Cover the [[Masa|masa]] with 2 slices each of the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Onions|onions]] and [[Peppers|peppers]].\n| Place 3 [[Mint leaves|mint leaves]] and a teaspoon of [[Rice|rice]] on the top.\n| Push [[Chilli|chilli]] slices into the edges of the [[Masa|masa]] and pour a teaspoon of the [[Marinade|marinade]] over the top.\n| To wrap, fold both ends of the [[Foil|foil]] or husks to the centre, allowing an overlap of 1 cm.\n| Fold one end tightly, stand the parcel on its end and shake down.\n| Tighten the wrapping and fold over the sides and seal.\n| The [[Tamale|tamale]] should be about 13 cm by 9.5 cm.\n| Repeat the process to make the remaining 7 [[Tamales|tamales]].\n| Place the [[Tamales|tamales]] in a large pan so that they are all in one layer.\n| Add cold water to cover.\n| Cover the pan and on a high heat, bring to the [[Boil|boil]], reduce heat, and [[Simmer|simmer]] for about 4 hours.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe as a snack, [[Light lunch|light lunch]] or even for breakfast.\n===Chef's notes===\nTamale flour, which is slightly more granular than masa harina can be obtained from [[Cool Chile Co]].  They also sell corn husks.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Tamales]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Tamales]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Tamales]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes|Tamales]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Tamales]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Tamales]]\n[[Category:Starters|Tamales]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Fruit recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#masa #tamales #tamale #orange #potato #mintleaves #onions #sevilleorange #tomatoes #foil #rice </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Pachamanca in olla",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pachamanca in olla, Ecuadorian recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#meats #corn #pachamancainolla #favabeans #potatoes #marinade #groundblackpepper #huacatay #sweetpotatoes #cornhusks #chincholeaves \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Pachamanca is the Quechua language word for a traditional Andean cooking technique, in which vegetables and meats are placed underground with very hot\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 11661\n|PortionCalories = 1457\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = Pachamanca being cooked traditionally\n |Servings = Serves 8\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 6 hours\n |PrepTime = 5 hours\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Pachamanca in olla recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n}}\n\nPachamanca is the Quechua language word for a traditional Andean cooking technique, in which [[Vegetables|vegetables]] and [[Meats|meats]] are placed underground with very hot stones and slowly [[Roasted|roasted]].  (\"Pacha\" means \"earth\", and \"manca\" means \"pot\" in Quechua). To prepare it you need some open space. When you don't have it, you can prepare pachamanca in olla. It is cooked over the fire in a clay pot.\n\n'''Note:'''  for the pachamanca - you can have one [[Meat|meat]], two [[Meats|meats]], or more!!!\n\n'''[[Meats|meats]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 900 g (2 lb) [[Lamb]] chops\n| 900 g (2 lb) [[Pork chops]]\n| 900 g (2 lb) whole [[Chickens]], quartered\n| 8 [[humitas]]\n| 2 cups [[Marinade]] Mixture\n}}\n'''[[Marinade|marinade]] mixture (2 cups)'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 cups [[Chicha]] de Jora\n| 1 [[Cilantro]] stems and leaves ([[coriander]]).  (Approx. 200 g)\n| 2 tbsp. Raw [[Garlic]] Paste\n| &#189; cup [[Huacatay leaves]]\n| &#188; cup [[Chincho leaves]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]] to taste\n}}\n'''[[Tubers|tubers]], [[Legumes|legumes]] and [[Corn|corn]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 450 g (1 lb) [[Fava beans]], in pods\n| 8 [[Corn|corn]] in the husks\n| 450 g (1 lb) [[Sweet potatoes]], whole\n| 450 g (1 lb) [[Potatoes]], whole\n| [[Salt]] and [[Ground black pepper|ground black pepper]], to taste\n}}\n'''garnish'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 2 cups of [[Aj\u00ed Amarillo Paste|Aj\u00ed Amarillo Paste - ''recipe here'']]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Blend]] all of the ingredients for the [[Marinade|marinade]]. Pour over [[Meats|meats]] and [[Marinate|marinate]] for 4 hours.\n| Soak the [[Fava beans|fava beans]], [[Tubers|tubers]], and [[Corn|corn]] in water for 1 hour.\n| Place a layer of [[Corn husks|corn husks]] in the bottom of the pot.\n| Place the [[Marinated|marinated]] [[Meats|meats]] over the layer of [[Corn husks|corn husks]], and then cover with a layer of [[Potatoes|potatoes]], [[Sweet potatoes|sweet potatoes]] and [[Corn|corn]]. Place a second layer of meats on top and continue layering the [[Potatoes|potatoes]], corn and finally the [[Fava beans|fava beans]]. \n| Cover the pot tightly and cook over a high flame for 35 minutes. Remove the clay pots from the stove and let the pachamanca rest for another 10 minutes.\n| Serve with [[Aj\u00ed Amarillo Paste]] or with [[Salsa criolla]]\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\n[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] has kindly done the following research into UK equivalents for some of the more difficult to obtain ingredients in this recipe.   Thank you Julia!\n* [[Huacatay]] is a type of marigold and seeds can be obtained from:  '''[http://www.chilternseeds.co.uk/item_1222d_tagetes_minuta_seeds Chiltern Seeds]'''.  Looks like they kill off weeds as well!\n* [[Chicha de Jora]] is a bit trickier as it is a drink made from [[sweetcorn|corn]].  There is a recipe for making it [http://www.ehow.com/how_2099371_make-chicha-de-jora.html here] , but I would suggest substituting it with a slightly sweetish [[white wine]].\n* [[Chincho leaves]] - I think they will be impossible to get here.  Seems they are related to [[huacatay]] and used to be used to treat malaria.  I wonder if our friend can come up with a substitute.\n* [[Fava beans]].  [[Broad beans]] in pods are not often available, so most of the year, it would have to be frozen and I presume we should allow for that when giving a weight.\n\n\n''Thank you to our Peruvian visitor, Gloria Sebastiani for kindly providing this recipe''\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Not able to try this out</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">2.5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nowhere near me I can dig a fire pit to do this. A shame.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilean recipes]]\n[[Category:Ecuadorian recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Peruvian recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Lamb recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#meats #corn #pachamancainolla #favabeans #potatoes #marinade #groundblackpepper #huacatay #sweetpotatoes #cornhusks #chincholeaves </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

Add this sauted ingredients to the previous sauce and blend until smooth. At the end add a little oil to make it brighter.\n| Make a bed of [[Lettuce|lettuce]] leaves on a large plate.\n| Place the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] on the top and pour the [[Sauce|sauce]] over them.\n| Sprinkle with the [[Sweetcorn|sweetcorn]] and [[Olives|olives]] and arrange the [[Eggs|eggs]] on the top.\n|\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\n[[Aj\u00ed pepper|Aj\u00ed amarillo]] chillies are available from the [[South Devon chilli farm|South Devon Chilli Farm]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Peruvian recipes]]\n[[Category:Potato recipes|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Starters|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Papas a la huancaina]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#papasalahuancaina #potatoes #cayennepepper #lemonjuice #turmeric #sweetcorn #olives #chillies #lettuce #boil #boiling </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

#tomatoes #onions #portsalut #tetillacheese #cream #papaschorreadasalacolombianapotatoesincheeseandchillisauce #fry \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A rich dish from Colombia., see ''see [[Talk:Papas chorreadas a la colombiana (Potatoes in cheese and chilli sauce)|comments]]''\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 50 minutes\n |PrepTime = 10 minutes\n |CookTime = 40 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Papas chorreadas a la colombiana recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Cheddar Colombia.\n, ''see [[Talk:Papas chorreadas a la colombiana (Potatoes in cheese and chilli sauce)|comments]]''\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 kg [[Potatoes|potatoes]] \n| 40g [[Butter|butter]]\n| 1 green [[Chilli|chilli]], finely chopped\n| 1 red [[Chilli|chilli]], finely chopped\n| 2 [[Onions|onions]], [[Diced|diced]] \n| 2 [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Skinning tomatoes|skinned]] and chopped\n| 125ml [[White wine|white wine]]\n| 150ml [[Double cream|double cream]] \n| 200g of [[Monterey Jack cheese]], [[Grated|grated]] or cubed \n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]] to taste\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Cheese and chili potatoes cream.jpg|Stir in the cream and cheese\nImage:Cheese and chili potatoes toms.jpg|Wine and tomatoes, reducing\nImage:Cheese and chili potatoes ingredients.jpg|Ingredients (about 1/2 quantity)\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Peel and [[Boil|boil]] the [[Potatoes|potatoes]].\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a pan and gently [[Fry|fry]] the [[Chillies|chillies]] and [[Onions|onions]] until the latter are soft.  \n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and [[Wine|wine]] cook for a further 5 minutes or so until the [[Sauce|sauce]] has reduced.\n| Stir in the [[Cheese|cheese]] and the [[Cream|cream]] and cook until the cheese has melted slightly.\n| Season to taste.\n| Serve the [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and pour the [[Sauce|sauce]] over them.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nGood with [[Salad|salad]] or [[Meat|meat]] or just as a snack.\n===Variations===\nIf liked, add finely diced or crushed garlic when frying the onions.\n\nNext day, the leftovers were mashed and grilled in an oven proof dish so the top was browned and crunchy, delicious. \n===Chef's notes===\nI would recommend a softish [[Cheese|cheese]] such as [[Port Salut]] or [[Tetilla Cheese|Tetilla]].\n\n--[[User:JuliaBalbilla|JuliaBalbilla]] 09:51, 13 January 2009 (UTC)\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Potatoes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Potatoes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes|Potatoes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes|Potatoes]]\n[[Category:Latin American                 "revisions": [
                    {

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Pato asado estilo la selva Roast duck jungle style Main course recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#duck #bayleaves #turmeric #garlic #plantain #cumin #stock #nutmeg #grated #corn #sauce \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This recipe comes from the city of Iquitos in Peru\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 627\n|PortionCalories = 78\n|DatePublished=1st February 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 8\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:The Jungle.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Peruvian roast duck</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Jungle stylee \ud83d\udc06 \ud83e\udd86 \ud83e\udd81</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis recipe comes from the city of Iquitos in Peru.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 [[Duck|duck]] weighing 1.8 kg, skin loosened and [[Fat|fat]] removed, and cut into 8 pieces; ''See here for a [[Jointing a chicken|similar procedure]]''\n| 2 tablespoons [[Corn|corn]] [[Oil|oil]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Turmeric|turmeric]]\n| [[Garlic]], to taste, crushed\n| 2 [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]]\n| 2 teaspoons [[Salt|salt]]\n| A pinch of freshly [[Grated|grated]] [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]]\n| &frac12; teaspoon [[Cumin|cumin]]\n| 1 ripe large [[Plantain|plantain]], peeled and cut diagonally into 8 slices\n| 360 ml water or [[Stock|stock]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a large pan, [[Stir-fry|stir-fry]] the [[Duck|duck]] in the [[Oil|oil]] with the [[Turmeric|turmeric]] over a medium heat for 10 minutes.\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Bay leaves|bay leaves]], [[Salt|salt]], [[Nutmeg|nutmeg]] and [[Cumin|cumin]] and mix well.\n| Cover the pan and allow the [[Steam|steam]] to produce some liquid.\n| Add the [[Plantain|plantain]] and the water or [[Stock|stock]].\n| [[Simmer]], covered, over a low heat for about an hour, until the [[Duck|duck]] is tender and there is a small amount of [[Sauce|sauce]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe warm, with rice and [[Salsa criolla]].\n===Variations===\nYou could try this recipe using any firm-fleshed [[Meat|meat]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pato asado estilo la selva (roast duck jungle style)]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Pato asado estilo la selva (roast duck jungle style)]]\n[[Category:Main courses|Pato asado estilo la selva (roast duck jungle style)]]\n[[Category:Peruvian recipes|Pato asado estilo la selva (roast duck jungle style)]]\n[[Category:Poultry recipes|Pato asado estilo la selva (roast duck jungle style)]]\n[[Category:Stews and casseroles|Pato asado estilo la selva (roast duck jungle style)]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#duck #bayleaves #turmeric #garlic #plantain #cumin #stock #nutmeg #grated #corn #sauce </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

-->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 518\n|PortionCalories = 129\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 3 hours 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 3 hours 15 minutes\n |CookTime = None\n |Image = [[Image:Pebre chileno recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Nioce and hot</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">\ud83c\udf36\ud83c\udf36\ud83c\udf36</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is a spicy [[Salsa|salsa]] from Chile.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 large firm [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], peeled and [[Diced|diced]] \n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], peeled and [[Diced|diced]]\n| 2 hot green or [[Red chillies|red chillies]], [[Diced|diced]] and [[Seeds|seeds]] removed if desired \n| 3 tablespoons fresh [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]], finely chopped\n| 2 tablespoons flat leaved [[Parsley|parsley]], finely chopped\n| 4 Cloves [[Garlic|garlic]], finely chopped\n| 3 tablespoons [[Olive|olive]] or [[Corn|corn]] [[Oil|oil]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] or [[White wine vinegar|white wine vinegar]]\n| [[Salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a bowl, mix together the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Onion|onion]], [[Chillies|chillies]], [[Coriander|coriander]], [[Parsley|parsley]] and [[Garlic|garlic]].  \n| Mix with a dressing made from the [[Oil|oil]], [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]] or [[Wine vinegar|wine vinegar]], [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n| Allow to rest at room temperature for at least 3 hours before serving.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nIdeal with one of [[Chile]]'s national dishes Porotos Granados, which is a [[Bean|bean]] and [[Vegetable|vegetable]] [[Stew|stew]].  It would also be an excellent accompaniment for [[Meat|meat]].\n===Variations===\nSometimes the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] are left out and you can use all [[Parsley|parsley]] or all [[Coriander|coriander]].  Apart from that there are no traditional variations although the ratios do differ according to personal taste.\n===Chef's notes===\nIt can be difficult to decide which [[Chillies|chillies]] to use.  This recipe calls for [[Hot chillies|hot chillies]], but I would not go so far as to use 2 [[haba\u00f1ero chillies]], for example.  [[Serrano]] or [[jalape\u00f1o chillies]] would probably be about right.  I would advise that you taste any chillies before adding them to this or other recipes.\n==See also==\n* [[Chilli sauce|Many other chilli sauce recipes]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pepper sauce]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Pepper sauce]]\n[[Category:Chilean recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Pepper sauce]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Pepper sauce]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Pepper sauce]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#parsley #diced #tomatoes #coriander #chillies #garlic #onion #lemonjuice #unusualrecipes #redchillies #stew </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

Do not allow them to burn.\n| Lower heat and add the [[Garlic|garlic]], again, stirring all the time.\n| When the [[Garlic|garlic]] is golden, stir in  the [[Chipotle|chipotle]] paste and add the [[Sugar|sugar]].\n| Turn off the heat, but leave on the hob, shaking the pan until the [[Seeds|seeds]] are coated with the [[Sugar|sugar]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with the [[Lime|lime]] half, the [[Juice|juice]] of which should be squeezed over the [[Seeds|seeds]].\n===Variations===\n[[Chipotle]] paste is available from Waitrose, but if you cannot get it, use 2 teaspoons [[Dried|dried]] [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]] and a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] instead.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Seeds|seeds]] will stay fairly fresh if you store them in a [[Lock&Lock boxes|Lock&Lock box]], but do not add the [[Lime|lime]] until they are served.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Dry fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pepitaspicantes #pumpkinseeds #lime #garlic #chipotle #seeds #chilli #toasted #dried #chilliflakes #unusualrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
